Current Commentary

International Shipping Competition and Our Country's Self-Defense

— Ji

International shipping competition is intensifying due to the impact of the global economic downturn, and the Far East has also become a target for major powers to compete for. The US government has agreed to allocate 30 million US dollars to subsidize American company Dollar Line to build new ships and expand Far Eastern shipping. Japanese shipping company Nippon Yusen Kaisha is also rapidly catching up, planning to quickly complete its new plan for 200,000 tons of new-style express ships. Osaka Shosen Kaisha has also resumed the South China route since April, and has also added ships to the Japan-Shanghai line. Other shipping companies from Germany, France, Britain, Italy, the Netherlands, and Norway are all actively preparing and unwilling to fall behind. This spring, the British Cabinet passed the Shipping Subsidy Act to enable British foreign shipping companies to compete with foreign shipping. German Norddeutscher Lloyd also has a large-scale plan to develop Far Eastern shipping. Italy's Far Eastern Shipping Company, known for its developed business, is also transferring 33,000-ton passenger ships originally operating on the Atlantic route to the Europe-Asia line to strengthen its lineup and compete with Norddeutscher Lloyd. French Shipping Company and Norwegian Bao Lung Company are all urgently seeking to revitalize their businesses in order to cope with the intense competition and open a new record for Far Eastern shipping competition. Foreign ships already have a tendency to dominate in China, and under these circumstances, China's shipping industry will be greatly affected.

China's shipping power is inherently weak, and the reasons for its difficulty in developing are also extremely complex. First, major powers manipulate China's inland and coastal navigation rights through their political power. Second, foreign merchant ships compete with us with their strong capital, complete equipment, fast and stable speeds, and low freight rates. Third, domestic shipping companies fail to cooperate closely. Fourth, the existing ships are old, the equipment is simple, and the speeds are slow. Fifth, the government fails to provide sufficient substantial assistance to the shipping industry. Sixth, frequent natural disasters and wars affect the navigation of ships. With these six factors, coupled with the constraints of donations and taxes and the harassment of bandits, few of China's national shipping industries can avoid misfortune. Therefore, since last year, shipping on all routes has been extremely sluggish. Due to the large number of ships and small amount of cargo on the North China route, freight rates for each ship have fallen competitively, resulting in exhaustion and huge losses. Although business on the Yangtze River route has improved slightly since the completion of water and land transportation since last autumn, Japanese merchant ships have returned strongly and are encroaching day by day, causing a blow to China's shipping industry. Business on the South China routes, such as the Shanghai-Hong Kong, Shanghai-Guangdong, and Guangdong-Guangxi lines, has also been in a state of decline. Furthermore, due to the decline in business, the infighting and struggles between domestic shipping companies are also intensifying. If this continues, the situation is truly worrying.

The Ministry of Communications, in view of this, convened national shipping companies on March 20 last year to discuss proposals to promote the shipping industry. Although there were more than 200 proposals, the most important of which was the case of shipping cooperation. At that time, it was decided that the Ministry of Communications would lead the Shanghai Shipping Association and the state-owned China Merchants Group to jointly form the China Shipping Design Committee to establish a complete shipping policy, so that the fragmented shipping industry would be forced by the needs of the environment to implement sincere unity.

Now, the China Shipping Cooperation Council will be established on May 1, and the cooperation plan has also been approved by the Ministry of Communications. It is reported that the main duties of the council are: (1) to adjust the shipping routes on the river and sea routes; (2) to balance the supply and demand of cargo space based on tonnage and frequency; (3) to realize the unity and cooperation of state-owned and private shipping; (4) to be open and transparent in everything and eliminate the harm of price reductions caused by mutual distrust. If the above-mentioned promises can be implemented one by one, then China's shipping industry, although in the midst of fierce competition, will have a chance to turn around in the future.

Although the fundamental cause of the decline of China's shipping industry does not lie entirely in the mutual fighting between companies, the unequal treaties relied upon by major powers to carry out organized and planned shipping aggression against us also have a great relationship. Therefore, how to recover the navigation rights of foreigners in China is also something that the entire country should pay attention to.

Roosevelt Issues Another Order to Increase Domestic Silver Price to 77.57 Cents per Ounce, Aiming to Protect American Interests, It Is Said That a Major International Reaction Is Gradually Occurring

(Washington) After President Roosevelt ordered tonight to increase the price paid by the government for domestically mined silver to 77.57 cents per ounce, silver-faction congressmen predicted one after another that the price of silver would soon rise to $1.29, or even exceed this number. (24th National Telegram)

(Washington) Bankers and silver brokers pointed out that the soaring world silver price was entirely caused by the activities of speculators such as India and the United States. They said that the policies of these countries are actually forcing the US government to raise domestic silver prices, giving speculators an extremely favorable position. It is heard that after the silver price soared to over 60 cents, the US Treasury Department has not purchased silver in the world market. It is estimated that the world's silver that can be immediately cashed is only 50 million ounces. Speculators now have no difficulty in quickly raising the silver price to above the government's newly set price. If you want to stop it, the only way is for the government to announce a temporary suspension of purchase or sale of silver. A major international reaction is gradually occurring. This matter not only has a further tightening effect in China, but also brews a serious situation in Mexico. The silver value of the Mexican currency itself is based on a silver price of 72 cents per ounce, which is equal to the circulating currency value of the Mexican currency. If the world silver price rises again, the Mexican silver coins will all be melted down. If so, the Mexican currency system will be greatly disrupted. If the Mexican government raises the exchange rate of its currency, Mexican trade will be adversely affected, especially trade with the United States. Bankers predict that the Mexican side will also strongly criticize the United States' silver policy, as will those from China. (25th Reuters Telegram)

(Washington) President Roosevelt issued an order this afternoon to increase the price paid by the government for domestically mined silver to 77.57 cents per ounce. This price increase was achieved by reducing the government's coinage tax from 45% to 40%. The president's action was quite sudden, because just a few hours ago, Treasury officials still stated that the government did not intend to raise the silver price again, and that the Treasury Department would give a price according to the world silver price when purchasing domestically mined silver in the New York silver market in the future. According to the president's order, this price increase will be implemented immediately. Beforehand, the Treasury Department suddenly held a meeting, completely reversing the attitude announced a few hours ago. The legal counsel to Treasury Secretary Morgenthau also attended the meeting. At that time, it was explained that, according to the London Silver Agreement, the US government must stockpile all of its domestically produced silver for currency purposes. Treasury officials apparently did not pay attention to this regulation in their statement a few hours ago. If the government purchases silver in the New York market, it is feared that the price of speculators will exceed the government price, so that the United States will not be able to fulfill the conditions of the London Agreement, so the president's order had to be issued. According to the government's recently set silver price, it is 71.11 cents per ounce, and the world silver price continues to rise, and this morning the New York market price has exceeded the government price. According to banker news, by this summer, the silver price has a tendency to rise to one dollar per ounce. (24th National Telegram)

(Washington) President Roosevelt today increased the price paid by the Treasury Department for domestically mined silver from 71 cents per ounce to 77.57 cents per ounce. This is the second increase in the domestic silver price this month. The first price increase was on April 10, from 64.5 cents to 71 cents, totaling a strong 13 cents in two weeks. President Roosevelt's order stated that this move was necessary for the sake of American interests. This statement was made in response to the recent surge in world silver prices. The coinage tax was originally levied at 45% of the silver currency price, which is $1.29 per ounce. Now, it is reduced to 40%. The Treasury Department may levy a 50% profit tax on the profits gained from the soaring silver price. This move aims to prevent domestic silver producers from hoarding silver in anticipation of higher government prices and gaining excessive profits. Congressional silver faction congressmen and western mines were extremely excited by the news of this price increase. Silver faction congressmen still predict that the silver price will soon rise to $1.29, because the Treasury Department's silver purchase price has already increased, and the world silver price will also rise accordingly. American silver miners calculated their profits based on the difference between foreign and domestic silver prices, and estimated that they had gained a paper profit of $1,468,250 due to President Roosevelt's actions. (24th Reuters Telegram)

(Washington) The silver market here today was affected by the soaring US domestic silver price, and prices soared. The spot price is 34 pence 875, an increase of 2 pence 0625, because there are more speculative purchases and fewer sales. Today's silver price reached the highest point since October 30, 1924. Although the recent developments in the United States have excited speculators, gold and silver merchants have criticized the United States' policy. The United States has not recently purchased silver, so the rise in silver prices is entirely due to speculators' manipulation. They will work harder to raise prices in the future. Some say that the real purpose of the United States is not to purchase silver in the world market, but to encourage speculators to raise silver prices in order to appease domestic silver faction congressmen. According to experts, this situation will continue, and speculators will eventually be caught. At the same time, bankers and financiers are now paying close attention to the increasingly serious currency difficulties in China and the backlash from the soaring silver price in Mexico. (25th Reuters Telegram)

(London) According to official news today, silver transactions between brokers at the London Metal Exchange must be settled weekly. This method will be tested for three months. The Exchange Council also has the right to announce special settlements. The weekly settlement price is determined at the end of the first session on Wednesdays. The delivery date is Friday. No special settlements may be held on Saturdays. Exchange brokers must make the same agreement with their customers. The first week's settlement price will be announced on May 8. Copper and tin are settled daily, and those delivered on Saturdays must be settled one day earlier, and those delivered on Sundays will be settled on the next day. Brokers can settle with the exchange weekly in accordance with the methods agreed upon with their customers, or with a minimum deposit of 10%. (24th Reuters Telegram)

(Paris) The "Capital" weekly magazine commented on the silver market situation, saying that the rise in silver prices only affects the foreign exchange market in the Far East, causing the currencies of silver-using countries in the Far East to rise against the US dollar. It also said, "Generally, when the silver price rises to 71.11 cents per ounce, the US government will raise the official purchase price again. The purpose of the US government is obviously to increase the international value of the currencies of the Far East and South American countries and restore silver to the status of a remittance product. However, this policy has not yet been officially announced." (24th Havas Telegram)

(Tokyo) The official price of American silver has risen to 71.185 US cents, so the Suiyo-kai changed the silver price to 79.023 yen, an increase of 1.05 yen compared to the previous day. Furthermore, because the US government announced that it would increase it to 77.57 US cents starting today, it suspended sales in the afternoon. Tomorrow, it will increase the Japanese yen by three, five, or six yen. (25th Domei Telegram)

Chicago Grain Market Temporarily Suspended

Chicago The Chicago Grain Market, the world's largest grain market, is temporarily suspended today because the directors managing the market must study the situation of the dispute arising from the reorganization of the Rosenbaum Grain Company. Exchange lawyers claimed that it was unprecedented in history that the exchange was ordered by the court not to exercise its powers under the exchange's regulations for handling broker bankruptcy. The exchange later announced that all Rosenbaum Company's accounts with the clearinghouse must be closed and settled, and that the company may no longer trade. (24th Reuters Telegram)

Wireless Radio Transmission of Images, Paris Begins Receiving and Sending Tonight

Franco-Russian Pact Negotiations Revived, Soviet Union Understands France's Position, Another Method Is Planned So That Both Sides Can Accept It, Laval to Go to Russia in May to Complete Procedures

(Paris) Prime Minister Flandin and Foreign Minister Laval have recently returned to Beijing after the Easter holiday. According to reliable sources, the obstacle to the Franco-Russian negotiations, namely the issue of the two countries automatically providing military assistance to each other, is now being negotiated again, and it will soon be mature. (25th National Society Telegram)

(Paris) The difficulties in concluding a military mutual assistance agreement between France and Russia have been resolved, and the agreement may be signed within days. This news is the main point of the announcement issued by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs today. Foreign Minister Laval will also go to Moscow on May 6 to complete all the procedures. As for how the currently planned method differs from the original draft agreement, it has not been explained. According to reports, Soviet Russia once insisted that when either country is invaded by another country, the other country should immediately automatically provide military assistance. The French government has no objection to this point, but it is learned that Britain and Italy do not agree very much, which has made France hesitate. In Secretary Simon's mind, the only effective way to maintain peace in Europe is for the major Eastern European powers to assist each other when they are attacked by the air force of an armed country. Therefore, French Prime Minister Flandin convened French legal experts to study how to satisfy both Russia and France, and at the same time not offend Britain and Italy. It is learned that today's announcement that the agreement may be signed next week is the result of experts' research. (25th National Telegram)

(Paris) Regarding the issue of the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Pact, the two sides have been in dispute for many days and have not yet reached an agreement. According to a report in the Business Daily, "The Soviet Union previously requested that if either side is infringed upon by a third country, the mutual assistance system should be applied mechanically. In France, due to the original constraints of the Locarno Pact, it is argued that the Council of the League of Nations should be requested to convene a meeting first, and only after its approval can military assistance be given to the other party. Later, the French government proposed a compromise plan to the Soviet Union as a way to reconcile, arguing that when one of the contracting countries is infringed upon by a third country, it should request the Council of the League of Nations to convene a meeting. In other words, even if one of the contracting countries is infringed upon, it should be submitted to the Council for discussion, but if both contracting countries want to provide assistance to each other with strength, they do not have to wait for the Council to convene a meeting before doing so." (25th Havas Telegram)

(Moscow) The Franco-Russian agreement has recently been negotiated by the two countries, and some details have not yet been agreed upon. It is learned that if no unexpected events occur, the People's Committee (i.e., the Soviet Cabinet) will meet tomorrow to discuss the position taken by the Soviet Union on this issue. Furthermore, the impression gained by Havas reporter Lao after a private conversation with people familiar with Soviet foreign policy is that the future of the Franco-Russian agreement negotiations is, on the whole, not unfavorable, and that any difficulties are by no means insurmountable. It is expected that the Soviet Union will adopt a method that takes into account France's legitimate concerns as much as possible. France wants to harmonize the constraints it will take with the constraints already concluded by France. On the one hand, France hopes to stabilize the danger of German aggression in an appropriate way, and on the other hand, it also hopes to make it easier for Poland to participate in the Eastern European Non-Aggression Pact. The Soviet Union has fully understood this point of view of France. According to people familiar with Soviet foreign policy, the Franco-Russian agreement is not intended to surround Germany, but to unite friendly countries with peaceful determination to form a fully strong front, so as to resist German imperialism with a peaceful policy and curb its outward conflict. Moreover, the relationship between France and Poland has recently eased, and the Soviet Union is quite satisfied with this. However, what the Soviet Union has always insisted on is that there must be resolute action at present, and that the trivial circumstances arising from all future events should not be over-worried. According to past experience, whenever a serious conflict occurs, it is of little importance to consider all the subtle points of law everywhere. It is almost pedantic to make meticulous considerations on the law while the other party is willing to tear up the treaty. This conversation is quite representative of the views of the Soviet authorities. Furthermore, the Soviet newspapers are completely silent about the negotiations on the Franco-Russian agreement, for fear that publishing comments may hinder the progress of the negotiations. The Soviet Union has gentle feelings and does not want to act rashly, which can also be seen in this matter. (24th Havas Telegram)

Italian and French Convening: The Rome Nine-Nation Conference to Conclude a General Non-Interference Treaty and Draft Proposals for Seeking Opinions from All Parties

(Rome) The Stresa Conference of England, France, and Italy decided to convene a nine-nation conference of the Danube River countries in Rome. Various diplomatic preparations are now underway for this conference. Italy advocates holding the meeting in early June. Italy and France have jointly invited Austria, Yugoslavia, Germany, Czechoslovakia, Hungary, Poland, and Romania to participate. Each participating country will send its foreign minister to attend. The main purpose of the conference is to seek common respect for Austria's independence and territorial integrity. The approach is divided into two types: (1) concluding a general non-interference in internal affairs treaty; (2) agreeing on sanctions in the event that the above treaty is violated. Regarding the non-interference treaty, it is reported that a draft has been prepared and sent to relevant countries for study. So far, most countries have accepted the draft. Poland and Hungary have only expressed acceptance in principle. Germany has requested a more precise interpretation of the term "non-interference in internal affairs." As for the methods of sanctioning violations of the treaty, relevant countries will separately conclude agreements within the framework of the League of Nations. These agreements can take the form of mutual assistance pacts and should be bilateral rather than multilateral. If all invited countries participate in the Danube River Conference and all participating countries conclude such bilateral agreements with each other, a total of thirty-six agreements could be concluded. However, some countries, such as Poland, may only accept the non-interference treaty and be unwilling to adopt other restrictions, which is also unknown. In addition, the issue of rearmament of Austria, Hungary, and Bulgaria can also be usefully discussed in Rome, but not in formal meetings. This is because the Danube River Conference has not formally included this issue on the agenda. According to the decision of the Stresa Conference, the issue of rearmament in Central Europe should be seriously considered only after a general and regional security guarantee solution has been agreed upon. Therefore, this issue can only be discussed informally in Rome to initiate a solution and ultimately be submitted to the League of Nations for resolution. (Havas dispatch, 24th)

Germany Requests Five Clarifications

(Rome) Although the intended goals of the nine-nation Danube River Conference are limited to guaranteeing Austria's independence and territorial integrity, it has already raised various issues during the preparatory meetings. Diplomatic authorities are now trying to resolve them before the conference begins. Germany previously sent a note to the French and Italian governments, stating that the Danube River Pact proposed in the Rome Agreement of January 7 lacked clarity. It specifically raised these questions and requested detailed explanations: (1) Switzerland is Austria's neighbor, why was it not invited to join the Danube River Pact in the Rome Agreement? Moreover, the UK's interests in Central Europe are no less than France's, why was the UK not invited to participate? The Italian government replied that Switzerland is a permanently neutral country and cannot sign mutual assistance pacts. The UK is unwilling to adopt other restrictions besides the Locarno Pact, so it was not invited to join the Danube River Pact. (2) If the Danube River Pact is signed, will the agreement between the UK, France, and Italy to consult each other in the event of a violation of Austria's independence (the Anglo-Franco-Italian declaration of September 27 last year) remain in effect? Italy replied that if all relevant countries, including Germany, join the non-interference treaty, then this consultation can be terminated. (3) Is the non-interference treaty limited to agreeing not to interfere in internal affairs, or must signatory countries also approve a mutual assistance pact? Italy replied that signatory countries should conclude special agreements to protect the principles of the non-interference treaty, but whether or not to sign is still up to each country to decide. (4) What is the precise meaning of "non-interference in internal affairs"? Italy replied that the Franco-Italian Rome Agreement of January 7 provided an explanation: each signatory country agrees not to encourage or support any incitement or propaganda that aims to undermine the territorial integrity and political and social systems of the signatory countries. (5) What role will the League of Nations play after the Danube River Pact is implemented? Italy replied that the League of Nations' task will naturally be in accordance with the provisions of the League of Nations Covenant. The above is the Italian government's explanation. After receiving the Italian reply, Germany found the explanations for the first, second, and third questions satisfactory, but raised objections to the answers to the last two questions. The German ambassador to Italy, Mr. Hassell, is said to have inquired of the Italian government in a private capacity whether it would violate the principle of non-interference in internal affairs if the Austrian government requested foreign military assistance to maintain its position. In addition, there are many other issues that need to be studied, the most important of which is the final resolution of the dispute between Hungary and Yugoslavia regarding the assassination in Marseille. As for the issue of Hungarian rearmament, it must wait until a Central European security system is established before it can be implemented. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

British Prime Minister Publishes Article Criticizing Germany's Treaty-Breaking Actions, Hoping to Implement the Three-Nation Resolution to Prove Peaceful Intentions

(London) The National Labour Party's organ published an article by Prime Minister MacDonald today on the situation in Europe, stating that the essence of all of Germany's actions stems from a rational background. The talks in Berlin indicated several points that need further study to contribute to a collective security system. However, the manner of Germany's actions has damaged the sentiment of mutual trust in Europe. Germany has destroyed the path to peace and filled it with terror. Germany's plan to demand military force will subject most European countries to its whip. Leaving aside honor and debate, how can Germany claim to be blind to the impact of its vast military buildup on the security of other countries? Germany may answer, "You must trust me, I have no designs on you." Germany was the safest country in Europe until it aroused fears that were detrimental to itself. Now it asks other countries to accept its verbal vows of peace, which it has not accepted from its neighbors. It is excessive for the German people to ask countries to recognize the legitimacy of their aims and means without the slightest suspicion by those who know them best. The door to an honorable solution is still open. Will Germany immediately announce its readiness to participate in making the resolutions of the Stresa Conference effective, thereby proving its peaceful intentions? (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Germany Does Not Forget Old Colonies: Memorials Held Simultaneously in Berlin and Africa

(Berlin) On April 24, 1884, Bismarck placed the land owned by the Bremen merchant Lüderitz in Southwest Africa under the protection of the German government, marking the beginning of German colonies. Today, the fifty-first anniversary is being held here. Members of the German Colonial Society and the Colonial Warriors Association are wearing old colonial uniforms and placing wreaths at the monument to Bismarck, the founder of German colonies. Former personnel of the German colonies in Southwest Africa are also holding the fiftieth anniversary of the appointment of Dr. Hintrager as the German official in charge of the Southwest African protectorate. This shows that the Germans have not forgotten their lost colonies. (Reuters dispatch, 24th)

U.S. Navy Reorganizes Fleet and Replaces Asian Flagship, Japan Believes it Has Great Significance, Pacific Maneuvers to Begin

(Nanjing) According to a dispatch from Washington, the U.S. authorities announced three military plans on the 19th, which can indicate the U.S. Navy's operational policy in the Pacific. One is the plan for a North Pacific air exercise, the second is to improve the various facilities of the army and navy in the Panama Canal, and the Senate Military Committee will appoint a special committee to study the issue of restricting railway employees in the canal zone to those with U.S. citizenship. The third is to incorporate the Asiatic Fleet flagship Augusta (10,000 tons, equipped with 8-inch guns) into the United Fleet, and replace it with the light cruiser Omaha (7,000 tons, equipped with 6-inch guns) as the Asiatic Fleet flagship. This plan is most noteworthy, because if war breaks out between Japan and the U.S., the Asiatic Fleet will inevitably be a sacrificial fleet, so it is advisable to have a light cruiser with very high speed as the flagship. The Augusta and other 14 first-class cruisers are divided into three teams to prepare the wheel formation adopted by the U.S. fleet when crossing the Pacific. (Nichi-Ren dispatch, 25th)

(Washington) The House debated the naval budget bill today. Democratic Congressman Maverick issued a warning, saying that the United States' plan to expand its navy may become an obstacle to world peace. The bill was passed by the Appropriations Committee yesterday, with a total budget of $465,286,261 after the committee reduced it by $15 million, an increase of $174,879,098 compared to the previous budget. Mr. Maverick recently proposed a non-war proposal, advocating that the U.S. army and navy should only be used for self-defense and prohibiting the U.S. from lending to other countries during wartime. Mr. Maverick said that he had conducted a detailed study before submitting the bill and had discussed it in advance with many international law experts. However, the bill is not intended to direct U.S. foreign policy, but its main purpose is to prevent the U.S. from being drawn into the vortex of conflicts in other countries. As for the future of the naval budget bill, although there is some opposition at present, observers expect that it will be able to pass both houses safely. According to reliable sources, the bill has been supported by President Roosevelt, Navy Secretary Swanson, and Democratic leaders in Congress. At the same time, the entire U.S. fleet has been concentrated in the areas of San Diego and Saint Peter, preparing to set off for maneuvers. The Navy Secretary announced that the first few days of the maneuvers will be held along the coast. On May 3, 153 warships will sail into the open ocean. By the time the fleet arrives in the Hawaiian Islands in late May, the main maneuver plan will be realized. It is currently tentatively scheduled that the fleet will maneuver in Hawaii for about a week, and then return to San Diego to participate in the California Pacific International Exposition. (Kuo-Min dispatch, 24th)

Germany Actively Rearming its Navy, Actively Proceeding with Shipbuilding Program, Adding Large Cruisers and Submarines

(London) The Morning Post published an article yesterday expressing concern about Germany's rearmament of its navy. Today, the Daily Telegraph also published an editorial, which said, "Germany will hold a memorial for the Battle of Jutland on May 31 (the great battle between the British and German navies in the Jutland Strait during the European War). The German government will also issue a formal statement at that time to explain the main points of its naval policy and shipbuilding plan. Currently, Kiel, Wilhelmshaven, Hamburg, and Bremen are openly preparing for shipbuilding. It is reported that the government has promised the shipyard in Hamburg alone to give it 40,000 tons of shipbuilding work this year." The Daily Telegraph predicted that Germany's shipbuilding program will include cruisers and submarines, and that cruisers will be divided into two types: one weaker than the French armored cruiser Dunkerque (26,500 tons displacement, 30 knots speed, equipped with eight 13-inch guns), and one larger than the existing German cruisers Karlsruhe and Leipzig (6,000 tons displacement, 32 knots speed, equipped with nine 6-inch guns), and its armament is also stronger. As for the tonnage of submarines, although it is similar to that of foreign new submarines, in terms of engine weapons and range of activity, it far exceeds them. The Daily Telegraph concluded that when the European War Peace Treaty was signed in 1919, Germany had about 700 young naval officers who were proficient in submarine piloting. Most of them are still under 40 years old. If they are appointed to the positions of submarine commander or instructor, they will certainly be able to do it well. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

Japanese Upper House Member Akaike Visiting China for Inspection

Nagasaki: Japanese Upper House member Akaike Koichi departed from Nagasaki for China today, planning to inspect the anti-Japanese sentiment and the results of the crackdown on boycotts of Japanese goods in various parts of China for three months. It is said that Akaike will travel to various places in South and North China. Akaike was the Superintendent-General of the Tokyo Metropolitan Police Department and is an Upper House member of the Seiyukai faction. (Hua-Lian News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Earthquake in Massachusetts, 32 Times in One Night, People Felt Like They Were on a Rocking Bed Indoors, Residents Rushed Outdoors, Fortunately No Deaths or Injuries, Cause is Said to be Changes on the Seabed

Provincetown, Massachusetts: This small town experienced 32 earthquakes tonight. Thousands of residents, like frightened birds, gathered in the streets. Fortunately, there were no deaths or injuries. During the earthquake, the houses shook, the picture frames on the walls creaked, and people felt like they were on a rocking bed indoors. According to geologists from Harvard University, the 32nd earthquake was the most violent. During the earthquake, many people did not have time to put on their clothes and fled into the streets for safety. When the fear subsided, the residents returned to their bedrooms. Experts from Harvard University said that the tremors were pervasive and that the epicenter was on the seabed 25 miles away. The cause of the earthquake may be changes in the geology of the seabed. (Kuo-Min News Agency dispatch, 24th)

Moscow City Cracking Down on Street Child Beggars, Police Searching Everywhere and Arresting More Than a Thousand

(Moscow) The Moscow municipal authorities have recently launched a large-scale operation to clear child beggars in the city. These child beggars wander around, without clothes or food, and their situation is very pitiful. They have become the most serious problem in Soviet society. It is said that within the past three weeks, the Moscow police have searched everywhere and arrested 1,202 homeless children. The whereabouts of the parents of some of them have been found, and they were immediately sent home, and their parents were warned that they should be responsible for supporting their children. The number of cases where parents were reprimanded by the police for ignoring the lives of their children reached as many as 11,300. Child beggars who are arrested and whose families cannot be found are sent to public institutions for foster care. (Kuo-Min News Agency dispatch, 24th)

At the expiration, the sales will be checked, and if continued exemption is necessary, it will be reviewed. However, as for the two types of dyke donations listed in the original consultation, the question of whether they should be exempted at the same time concerns the scope of the Economic Commission, and a letter has been sent to discuss it. Bond Provision of Guarantee, Handling Methods for Various Courts

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Justice, according to the presentation of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the consultation request of the Ministry of Finance, ordered all courts that, when parties to a lawsuit provide guarantees with public price treasury bonds, they should accept them in accordance with the law. The department has now adopted the method stated by the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court and issued a notice to all courts to refer to it for handling. The methods are: (1) Public debt treasury bonds provided as guarantees or security deposits, except where the court determines that the situation requires the payment of cash, will be accepted; (2) The public debt treasury bonds provided are limited to those that have been consolidated by the National Government. Those with excessively fluctuating market prices will not be accepted; (3) The bonds provided shall be converted into amounts based on the market price of the stock exchange on the day before the submission of the case, and shall not be offset by the face value. If there is no market price for the bonds on the stock exchange, and there is indeed a price, it shall be consulted with the silver and money industry and converted according to its buying and selling price; (4) When the market price of securities falls, the payers shall be ordered to pay the full amount in accordance with the law; (5) The expenses for entrusting the bank to keep them shall be borne by the person paying the bonds, and the interest earned shall still belong to the payer, but shall be accumulated and deposited, and shall be jointly claimed when the securities are returned. (Central News Agency dispatch, 25th)

Abolition of Silk Cocoon Transit Tax

(Nanjing) The Wuxi Silk Factories Association petitioned for exemption from the silk dual tax. The Ministry of Finance had previously approved that domestic sales of local goods, without reporting transit through customs, should be subject to transit tax as usual, not a special tax levied on silk cocoons. Cocoons previously purchased were mostly produced in the county, and because they did not pass through customs, no tax was paid, thus misunderstandings were inevitable. Now, the Ministry has requested the abolition of this transit tax, and the Central Political Council has approved the implementation date. All transit taxes that the association should pay for purchasing cocoons from provinces such as Zhejiang, Shandong, Anhui, and Hubei, will naturally be abolished uniformly. (25th Special Dispatch)

International Commercial Telegram April 25th Reuters Special Commercial News

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today is 144 shillings and 5 pence, up 8 and a half pence.

London Large Bars: As generally expected, the US Department of Agriculture today increased the domestic new mine silver price to 77.57 cents per ounce. Silver prices here rose sharply, reaching the highest record since October 1925. Today's spot price is 34.875 pence, and the futures price is 35 pence, both surging 2.0625 pence. The market was quite turbulent in the morning, but the trend was quite firm. It is said that China sold and speculators bought when the price rose. It has now broken out again, and the price has risen. The market situation at the close of trading is uncertain.

Mountri Large Bars: Today's silver market price surged, rising by 300 pounds, expressing sympathy for London and New York.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was quite mixed this morning. The opening price for British-American exchange was $4.8375, lower than yesterday's US-British closing price by 0.0125. Prices fell before 11:00 AM, then rebounded slightly. The price at 2:00 PM in the afternoon was $4.831875, lower than the opening price by 0.04375.

British-French: Continental Europe continued to sell pounds, causing the franc price to rise this morning. The opening price for the French exchange was 73.34 francs, lower than yesterday's closing price by one pound. The exchange rate fell in the morning, then rebounded slightly. The price at 2:00 PM in the afternoon was 73.22 francs, lower than the opening price by twelve pounds.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: New York cotton market opened higher, the market situation was stable. Recently, someone made up for it. It is said that there is little certified cotton on hand.

British Cotton: Liverpool cotton market continued to show a stable atmosphere today. The July futures price at 1:00 PM in the afternoon was 6.37, higher than yesterday's closing price by one pound.

American Wheat: Chicago wheat market was turbulent and uncertain, so there was not much change in opening. Due to rain in the wheat area, prices loosened. It is heard that the Rosenbaum Company incident involved no more than 500,000 bushels, and it is expected to be cleared up.

British Wheat: Liverpool wheat market continued to loosen this morning. The July futures price at 1:00 PM in the afternoon fell 0.75 to 5 shillings and 6.75 pence.

Rubber

London: The rubber market situation was loose today. The transaction price for the July and September futures was 5.75 pence, down 0.0125.

New York: Rubber is still sluggish. After opening today, there were few transactions and prices fell slightly. The sluggishness of foreign markets is also a factor in the sluggish trading here.

Securities

New York: The market prices for securities opened higher today. The boom in mining stocks was the most intense. Railway and airline stock prices were also firm. The general atmosphere in the morning was very stable, but steel stocks remained lagging behind. The New York securities market prices are listed on the left.

Public Telegram

The Shaanxi China Foreign Famine Relief Association begs the charity of all philanthropists forwarded by the Shen Bao. Shaanxi has suffered a devastating drought in recent years, and the assistance has been unforgettable. We earnestly hope that benevolent people will generously donate aid to save the survivors and show universal compassion. The telegram cannot express the urgency of the situation. The Shaanxi China Foreign Famine Relief Association respectfully reports.

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Orders the Rectification of Sichuan Province's Finances

Taking the Rectification of Finances in Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi as a Model

Instructing the Provincial Government to Forward to All Counties for Reference, Selection, and Implementation

Chongqing Correspondence: For the sake of rectifying local finances in Sichuan Province, Chairman Chiang specially sent a fast mail telegram on the 20th, enclosing a compiled volume of the Regulations for Rectifying County Local Finances in Bandit Suppression Areas and related laws and regulations, ordering Provincial Chairman Liu to follow them. The original order is as follows: "To Chairman Liu of the Chongqing Provincial Government: Upon investigating the situation of local finances in various counties of Sichuan, it is found that due to the separation of defense zones in the past, the establishment of separate regimes, and the large number of local militias, all military, political, and militia expenses were arbitrarily demanded and freely apportioned locally. From military commanders to county magistrates, collection bureau chiefs, and village elders, all contrived names to carry out exploitation. Therefore, the annual collection of land tax in each county was carried out seven or eight times, or even more than ten times. The various other exorbitant taxes were even more numerous. Multiple taxes on one item and multiple levies on one tax were seen as the norm. Tax collectors and clerks followed each other to the people, and public and private checkpoints were everywhere. At the same time, there was no method of supervision or auditing for all collection and payment items within each county. Exaggerated collections, fabricated reports, embezzlement, and corruption were rampant. Even taxes that had been explicitly exempted were still privately collected by the responsible personnel. As a result, the people of each county, although exhausted by their contributions, were still unable to meet the various military, political, and economic expenses. The situation was precarious. The people suffered more than being hung upside down, and the authorities sat idly by, accumulating resentment, resulting in self-enrichment for corrupt local tyrants. This chaotic local finance phenomenon is unprecedented in any other province. Since the reorganization and establishment of the provincial government, the various military defense zones and political control have been voluntarily returned. Subsequently, the provincial government has been responsible for the overall planning and reduction of various exorbitant taxes and levies of the province's treasury and has begun to rectify them. However, the chaos of local finances in each county is even greater than that of the provincial finances. Without thorough reform measures, it will be impossible to alleviate suffering, eliminate accumulated evils, and achieve the practical results of rescuing the people and enriching the treasury. When I was supervising the bandit suppression in Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi, I specially formulated the Regulations for Rectifying County Local Finances in Bandit Suppression Areas, which were first implemented in the four provinces. As a result, the county local finances of each province became orderly and gradually entered the right track. The burden on the people was thereby reduced, and the local revenue and expenditure were suitable. Just taking the militia expenses of the two provinces of Henan and Hubei as an example, before the promulgation of these regulations, the annual expenses of each province ranged from 12 million to 15 million yuan, not including the expenses inflated and unaccounted for by those in charge. After the implementation of these regulations, the annual militia expenses of Henan and Hubei have been reduced to 4 million or 5 million yuan, and there is no possibility of any additional needs. Other expenditures are also roughly the same, and the results are remarkable, as can be seen in general. The main points of these regulations are: First, unify the agencies for various public funds. All county-owned public funds and public property income and expenditure matters in the county, such as education, militia defense, self-government, and charity, shall be handled by the finance committee established by the county government, implementing unified collection and unified expenditure, eliminating the past malpractices of divergent agencies, self-collection, self-expenditure, and scattered unaccountability. Second, strictly implement the budget and final account system. All county local additional taxes and other income, as well as all expense expenditures, shall be prepared in accordance with regulations, with budget and final accounts. Items already budgeted shall not be diverted for other purposes. Expenditures outside the budget, the use of reserve funds, and increases or decreases in taxes shall be rejected by the finance committee without the approval of the provincial government. Then, the abuses of indiscriminate spending, false consumption, and the free fundraising by institutions and groups in the local area will no longer be able to succeed. Third, divide the responsibilities of payment and management. The county magistrate holds the authority of payment, while the finance committee is responsible for the receipt and expenditure of all cash. The finance committee is also responsible for auditing whether the county budget and final accounts are appropriate and verifiable. At the same time, the county magistrate can still supervise and inspect the cash managed by the finance committee at any time. In addition, it is stipulated that the members of the finance committee must be just people from the urban and rural areas of the county, who will naturally attach importance to local funds. Therefore, with the separation of powers and mutual supervision between the finance committee and the county magistrate, it will not be difficult to gradually eliminate the past abuses of embezzlement, false reports, and misappropriation of public funds. All of these are the most effective ways to correct the chaos of local finances in various counties of Sichuan and are also the most effective measures for preliminary rectification. It should be known that county local affairs are the foundation of national administration and provincial administration, and county finance is the foundation of all county local affairs. If it is not followed in the right way and handled in an orderly manner, officials and people will inevitably be in distress and unable to cope. How can there be any administrative efficiency to speak of? The past situation in Sichuan can serve as a warning. This is not only something that the officials of the province should have a clear understanding of, but also something that the local people should have a thorough understanding of. Therefore, I have specially enclosed a compiled volume of the Regulations for Rectifying County Local Finances in Bandit Suppression Areas and related laws and regulations, and issued them by telegram. I hope that you will immediately order all counties to strictly implement them and supervise them closely. Do not deviate from them due to inaction. The origins of each county's revenue and expenditure items should also be transferred to fill in the forms for investigation and review within a limited time. In addition, the various chapters, rules, forms, and documents attached to the regulations, whether promulgated by the central government or established and implemented by other provinces, are all good rules for rectifying finances and effective methods for implementation. In particular, they should be referred to for selection and implementation in order to achieve perfection. I also request that you transfer the instructions for compliance and report the compliance situation for record. Chiang Kai-shek (April 20th, Secret, Calculated Enclosed One Volume of the Regulations for Rectifying County Local Finances in Bandit Suppression Areas and Related Laws and Regulations)" (Central News Agency, April 22nd)

Xiamen Various Circles Oppose Swire's New Pier —Water Transport Groups Also Have Disputes with Swire—

Xiamen Correspondence: The Xiamen branch of the British Swire Shipping Company was originally located in the most prosperous area of Haihoutan. When the former Municipal Office constructed Zhongshan Road, the company's location was deemed suitable for an intersection and urgently needed to be demolished and ceded. Yang Decong of Changyu Company, with the permission of Zhou Xingnan, the director of the Municipal Office, filled the new land in front of Tongwen Road and the right to build near the shore customs building, and sold it to Swire for 500,000 yuan in a perpetual lease. The Municipal Office received 100,000 yuan for the land price, and Yang received 400,000 yuan for the filling fee. This perpetual lease contract was signed by Swire, Yang Decong, and the Road Administration Office, and was officially sealed and established by successive Siming County magistrates Yang Tingshu and Xu Youchao after being sent to the British Consulate in Xiamen. Swire then used the land price from selling the old company address to pay the lease price and built the new pier and the customs bridge on Tongwen Road. Last year (1934), various circles in Xiamen opposed Swire's perpetual lease of the new pier and Lin Mutu, a Taiwanese citizen, purchasing land in Maohoushe, Heshan, to operate the Xiamen South Reclamation Company, and formed the "Committee Against Zhou Xingnan's Unauthorized Sale of National Land," which filed a complaint with the central government. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent treaty commissioner Liu Guangqian to Xiamen to investigate the entire case. After reporting back to Beijing, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs recently sent Lin Shaonan, the special inspector for Fujian and Zhejiang, to Fujian to be responsible for handling both cases. The construction of Swire's new pier and bridge was completed this month. In the future, Swire's northbound and southbound ships, as well as the Nanxiang, can directly dock, and passengers and goods can directly land. However, large and small ships in Xiamen Port all dock in the sea, and passengers and goods are transported by large ships and small boats. Therefore, workers who make a living from sea transport believe that the completion of Swire's new pier will have a significant impact. The Federation of Water Transport Groups has launched an opposition, and at the same time, the anti-Zhou association opposing the perpetual lease has also submitted a request to the central government, urging a speedy resolution to the case, arresting Zhou Xingnan and Yang Decong, canceling the contract according to the agreement, recovering the land valuation, and purchasing the new pier. The trend was very strong for a while. However, amidst opposition from all sides, Swire Company's writing room, comprador's office, and entire warehouse moved from the old site in Haihou to the new pier on Tongwen Road on the 23rd and officially opened for business on the same day. However, the consulate issued a message stating that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government and the special inspector for Fujian and Zhejiang had not recently delivered any negotiation documents regarding this case to the British Embassy in China or the Xiamen Consulate. Therefore, the British Consulate here is taking a silent attitude on this case. Swire's move to the new pier has obtained formal perpetual lease procedures from the local Chinese government. Although the public has reacted, there is no possibility of preventing the move unless the Chinese diplomatic authorities raise any objections or special circumstances arise. Moreover, with the completion of the new pier, the old pier has already begun to be demolished, and the agreement should be fulfilled. If the Chinese diplomatic authorities have any objections to this in the future, both parties can still resolve it peacefully. Moving in or not moving in will not be a problem, etc. As for the negotiation between the water transport groups and Swire, it is about the opposition to the flyover issue, which is a different matter from the opposition to the perpetual lease issue. It has been agreed with Swire that the proposed conditions will be temporarily implemented before Swire's London headquarters has signed and replied to all vessels, and will not dock at the new pier. This is the result of direct negotiation between the water transport groups and Swire. The Committee Against Zhou Xingnan's Unauthorized Sale of National Land sent another telegram to the Nanjing National Government on the 21st, insisting on the revocation of the agreement signed by Zhou and Swire, and the valuation of the buildings to be recovered by the government for use by domestic shipping companies to protect national rights. Wang Kuanshun, a farmer in Daijiamen Town, under the jurisdiction of the county, and his wife, Zhang, are both 65 years old. The citizens thought the case was bizarre and thousands of people came to watch the news. After Prosecutor Li took the seat on the scene, he summoned everyone for questioning and ordered the coffin to be opened. Furong's body had rotted. The teeth were found to be red, and there were wounds on the hands and feet. One tooth was broken on the left, and there was a hard wound on the waist. It was confirmed that he had been injured and died before his death. Yang'er's body was placed in a large cattail bag, with mud all over his body. He was first washed with water, and there were red spots all over his body, but no wounds. It was because he died of smallpox. After the coroner finished the examination, the prosecutor ordered Xiaolong to collect the remains, and the defendants were sent back to prison to await investigation.

Local News

Kong Arrives in Shanghai and Hopes that the People Will Love and Use National Loans and Not Buy a Large Number of Cheap Imported Goods Three Banks Distribute Huge Loans to Rescue Industry and Commerce

According to the Central News Agency, Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, left Beijing by night train at 11:00 p.m. the night before yesterday and arrived at Zhenru at 7:10 yesterday morning, and went straight back to his private residence on West Ames Road for rest. In the afternoon, he went to the Central Bank to handle important official matters and met with reporters to issue the following remarks:

I sincerely hope that the people will value the national currency.

According to Kong, it is well known that the United States' increase in the price of silver has affected our country. The reason is that our country does not produce silver and is a country with an import surplus. On the positive side, the price of imported goods should be cheaper than before. On the contrary, the price of exported goods must be more expensive, resulting in a decrease in export power. If imports increase on one side and exports decrease on the other side, the import surplus must be greater. Green international trade originally offset goods through exports. Now, the number of deficiencies is increasing, then the cash that we should pay for foreign goods is increasing. However, I hope that the people of our country will have patriotism, not seek profit, value the national currency, and not exchange it for foreign currency because it is cheap, which will cause the national currency to flow out, and strive to promote the use of domestic goods and not buy a large number of cheap imported goods, then this layer is not enough to be a problem.

The outflow of cash is not worth worrying about

As for the fear that our cash will flow out again due to the surge in silver prices, this is even less of a concern. Now, such as foreign bankers, have a long-term vision and hold a century-long plan. They have already negotiated cooperation with our financial circles and will not export silver. They will never only care about current interests and speculative transactions. This kind of behavior is really not taken by legitimate merchants with a long-term vision. Even if someone intends to sabotage, the government can increase the countervailing duty as an effective response as a last resort.

Three banks distribute 7-8 million

Then, regarding the relief of industry and commerce, now that the four bottoming difficulties have arrived, the suspicions of Zhongjiao and other banks' distribution have exceeded 7-8 million, and the market situation has been greatly stabilized. Yesterday's newspaper reported that the banking side of this matter is still waiting for the Ministry of Finance to designate candidates for the committee to handle the matter. This is a misreport. The United States Continues to Raise Silver Prices: Opinions from the Financial World; Our Nation Must Seek Its Own Way Out by Striving to Remedy the Trade Deficit

A Central News Agency report states that President Roosevelt, yielding to the opinions of pro-silver legislators, continues to vigorously promote the silver policy. Currently, silver prices everywhere are showing a consistent upward trend. According to the speculation of a certain prominent figure in the banking community here, this trend will have little impact on countries with trade surpluses, but will be extremely detrimental to countries with trade deficits. In the past, competition in the commercial arena was entirely based on tangible goods. This later evolved into the buying and selling of stocks. Now, the focus of transactional competition has shifted to intangible currencies. This is truly a distorted development in economics. The intensity of the currency wars among nations can be said to have reached its peak. However, the United States occupies a very important position in the world economy. Therefore, the impact of the US implementing the silver policy will be even greater than that of other countries. The reason why the United States is raising silver prices is, on the one hand, to show goodwill to pro-silver legislators. On the other hand, it also has implications for coping with a world war. If one can gain an economic advantage after a world war breaks out, that is even better than having a military advantage. Moreover, if silver prices are low, the economy will inevitably experience difficulties and tightness during wartime. Thus, the ease with which silver can be distributed, its turnover will be better than that of gold. Therefore, the United States disregards everything else to raise silver prices, implement its silver policy, and attempt to seize the leading position in the world economy, which is inevitable. Hence, the United States continuing to raise silver prices can be said to be a necessary trend. The adverse effects of the silver policy on our nation, and the hope that the United States will abandon the silver policy, are like seeking fish in trees. Currently, China must seek its own way out, and remedying the trade deficit is the most urgent task.

Minister Kong Will Crack Down on Intentionally Bankrupt Money Houses: Should Be Compensated According to Unlimited Liability Companies, and Those Disrupting Finance Will Be Punished

A Kuomin News Agency report from Shanghai on the 25th states that a reporter from the agency yesterday met with Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance to inquire about the state of the money industry. He was granted the following statement: Recently, after the Yongxing and Tongtai money houses successively declared bankruptcy, there was slight panic in the money industry. This was subsequently stabilized by the continued interbank lending of the Three Banks. From yesterday onwards, the situation has been steadily improving. Therefore, there should be no problems with the end of the April term. However, money houses in our country have always occupied an important position in finance. It is only because they have been accustomed to outdated organizational structures and have made few improvements that they have given cause for criticism. Unexpectedly, in recent times, there have been several money houses that, upon investigation, were actually not impossible to maintain, but have intentionally declared bankruptcy. They then perfunctorily deal with all creditor and debtor issues with a liquidator. Such behavior is tantamount to fraud and is a scourge on society, and should be strictly cracked down upon. If the above situation occurs again, in addition to being required to fully compensate creditors as an unlimited liability company, they should also be given punishments for disrupting finance. The manager of a money house is like the captain of a ship. If a storm is encountered, the captain must do everything possible to struggle. If the ship is beyond saving, the captain should be the last to abandon ship, thereby fulfilling their duty. However, recently, when money house managers encounter difficulties, they first try to evade responsibility. Some even abscond with funds. This situation is particularly hateful. In the future, the government will severely punish such behavior to warn the cunning and preserve the rights of depositors.

Two Loan Cases of 20 Million Yuan: Methods Can Be Determined This Morning; Shanghai Money Market Sets Inner Rate at 5.5 Yuan

A report from the Kuomin News Agency states that the end-of-April settlement period is fast approaching, and the market situation has gradually stabilized. Businesses can generally pass through this difficult period safely, and the methods for the two loan cases of 20 million yuan can also be determined by the Central Bank's board of directors after taking office today. The details are as follows:

Loan Methods to Be Determined Today

The measures for the mortgage loan of 15 million yuan and the small-scale industrial and commercial credit loan of 5 million yuan, organized by the Ministry of Finance, the Central, China, and Communications Banks, together with the Shanghai Bankers Association, have been drafted by Xi Demao of the Central Bank, Bei Songsun of the Bank of China, Zhang Peishen of the Bank of Communications, etc. They will be proposed at 10:00 AM this morning, taking advantage of the inauguration of the new board of directors of the Central Bank, for final discussion in order to start the process. The Central Bank bears more responsibility for the distribution of this loan (for example, in the 5 million yuan credit small loan, the Bank Association only contributes 1 million yuan from the Bank of China, 400,000 yuan from the Bank of Communications, and a total of 485,000 yuan from other banks. The remaining amount must be borne by the Central Bank). Moreover, the president of the bank is the Minister of Finance, so the final decision must be made by the bank.

There were no requests for interbank lending from the Central, China, and Communications Banks yesterday, except for applications for extensions and a small number of redemptions of mortgaged items. This is a sign that the money market is gradually stabilizing.

Money Industry Association: Agreed on Inner Rate

The Shanghai Money Industry Association convened its 38th Executive Committee meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon. (2) Regarding the order from the Social Affairs Bureau to open the inner garden, it was decided that the matter concerns the overall scope and should be submitted to the regular meeting of member representatives on May 2nd for discussion. Other motions were also discussed, and the meeting adjourned at around 3:00 PM.

As the end of April quickly approaches, collections and settlements are frequent, and credit is inevitably tighter. Yesterday, foreign rates rose by two points, both morning and afternoon, to 1.2 fen. According to a money industry insider who spoke to the reporter, it is difficult for the industry to make a uniform decision on extensions or settlements for the long-term settlement at the end of April. This matter can only be decided by each house based on its own circumstances and the situation of its debtors, and to separately decide whether to extend or settle.

Domestic and International Ship Radio Telegrams: To Be Started on May 1st

In order to develop domestic and international telegraph services, the Ministry of Communications has specifically launched ship radio telegrams. The charging rules have been approved and distributed to various telegraph offices for compliance. They will be simultaneously received and sent by the International Telecommunications Bureau, Telegraph Office, various post office telegraph receiving offices in the city, and various telegraph offices across the country, starting from May 1st. The details are as follows:

Telegram Rules

The Ship Radio Telegram Rules promulgated by the Ministry of Communications are recorded as follows: Article 1: Telegrams transmitted between ship radio stations and coast radio stations or other ship radio stations are called ship radio telegrams. Article 2: Ship radio telegrams are divided into the following two types: (1) Domestic ship telegrams (2) International ship telegrams. Article 3: Telegrams transmitted by ships that have been registered with the Ministry of Communications and issued a ship radio station license, and that travel to and from various places within the country, and that are relayed by various coast radio stations under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Communications, are domestic ship telegrams and are charged according to the provisions of Article 4. Ship telegrams that do not meet the above requirements are international ship telegrams and are charged according to the provisions of Article 5. Article 4: Domestic ship telegrams are charged in national currency and include the following: (A) Domestic rate (B) Coast radio station fee (C) Ship radio station fee (D) Surcharges for various special services. The domestic rate and coast radio station fee belong to the Ministry of Communications. The ship radio station fee belongs to the sending or receiving ship radio station. Surcharges for various special services belong to the Ministry of Communications or the ship radio station, respectively. Article 5: International ship telegrams are charged in gold francs (in the Republic of China, silver dollars are charged according to the gold franc to silver dollar rate stipulated by the Ministry of Communications) and include the following: A. Ship radio station fee, B. Coast radio station fee, C. Domestic telegraph line fee, D. International telegraph line fee, E. Surcharges for various special services. The ship radio station fee belongs to the sending or receiving ship radio station. The coast radio station fee belongs to the telegraph administration of the coast radio station to which the coast radio station belongs. The domestic telegraph line fee belongs to the Ministry of Communications. The international telegraph line fee belongs to the relevant national telegraph administrations. Surcharges for various special services belong to the Ministry of Communications or the ship radio station or other relevant telegraph administrations, respectively. Article 6: The price list for domestic and international ship telegrams will be set separately. Article 7: Domestic foreign language code telegrams are charged according to the price and are not subject to the international code telegram discount charging method. Article 8: The special services applicable to domestic and international ship telegrams are limited to the following six types: A. Prepaid reply fee, B. Verification, C. Distribution, D. Delivery notification (the date and time when the coast radio station transmits the telegram to the ship radio station is notified to the original sender), E. Special delivery (only applicable to telegrams sent from ships to land), F. Fee-paid public service telegrams. The surcharges for the special services in the preceding paragraph are charged according to the domestic telegraph rates for domestic ship telegrams and according to the international telegraph rates for international ship telegrams. Article 9: Domestic ship telegrams should have the word "Inradio" clearly marked at the beginning of the header to distinguish them. International ship telegrams should be handled in accordance with international radiotelegraph regulations. Article 10: For Chinese or foreign language telegrams sent from ships to land, the name and address of the recipient should be written in accordance with ordinary telegram methods. For Chinese or foreign language telegrams sent from land to ships, the recipient's name (and title should be clearly listed, and must be written in accordance with the following methods: (A) Recipient (and title or other necessary supplementary notes, (B) Ship name, (C) Name of the coast radio station through which the telegram is relayed. Example 1: Ding Zihong, Cabin 20, Xinming, Yantai. Example 2: Captain Wanghihlee S.SHaiyun Tsingtaoradio. The recipient's name, title, ship name, coast station name or address in domestic ship telegrams should be calculated according to the number of characters and are not subject to the rule of calculating 15 characters as 5 characters. Article 11: Ships stipulated in paragraph 1 of Article 3 of these rules that wish to apply the provisions of domestic ship telegram price list for telegrams to and from various places within the country should submit an application to the Ministry of Communications through their supervisory agency for approval and record, and then the Ministry of Communications will notify various coast radio stations and telegraph offices before it becomes effective. Article 12: The provisions of the international radiotelegraph regulations and the international telegraph regulations regarding ship telegram charges that do not conflict with these rules shall apply. Article 13: The provisions of these rules may apply to telegrams transmitted between aircraft radio stations and land radio stations. Article 14: These rules shall be implemented from May 1, 1935.

Price List

Domestic ship radio telegram price list (calculated in national currency) is divided into (1) Domestic rate: 1 jiao for clear Chinese or foreign language, 2 jiao for Chinese code or foreign language. (2) Coast radio station fee: 1 jiao for clear Chinese or foreign language, 2 jiao for Chinese code or foreign language. (3) Ship radio station fee: 5 fen for clear Chinese or foreign language, 1 jiao for Chinese code or foreign language. The total price for the above three items is 2 jiao 5 fen for clear Chinese or foreign language, and the total price for Chinese code or foreign language is 5 jiao. The price list for international ship radio telegrams is omitted.

Simultaneous Receipt and Sending

In order to complete domestic and international wireless telegraph services, the Ministry of Communications ordered all telegraph offices across the country to simultaneously receive and send domestic and international wireless telegrams starting from May 1 of this year, which are concurrently handled by the telegraph receiving and sending offices of various post offices and telegraph offices, with the International Telecommunications Bureau as the main organizer, and then sent by the Zhenru International Wireless Radio Station.

Our Authorities Will Urge the Siamese Government to Improve the Treatment of Overseas Chinese: Plan to Order Minister Jiang to Negotiate a Trade Treaty

A Central News Agency report states that various parties here are paying close attention to the various harsh regulations promulgated by the Siamese authorities for our overseas Chinese. It is reported that there are more than 3 million Chinese living in Siam, and the commercial relations between the two countries are also very close. In particular, the amount of Siamese rice imported into China each year is considerable. Siam's implementation of such harsh regulations on our overseas Chinese will not only have adverse effects on commercial relations between the two countries, but will also be extremely detrimental to the overall national relations. However, since the two countries are geographically adjacent and have very close ethnic relations, the Chinese living in that country have now formally requested the government authorities to use proper procedures to urge the authorities of that country to improve treatment. Therefore, in addition to making goodwill inquiries to the authorities of that country, our government authorities will also order Jiang Zuobin, the minister stationed in Japan, to be responsible for negotiating a trade treaty between the two countries, as the two countries have not yet established such a treaty, so as to establish proper relations between the two countries.
